# OpenAI Plugin - ElizaOS Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#content-area)

[ElizaOS Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/elizalabs/bbIJsUzCDybj9a-t/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=bbIJsUzCDybj9a-t&q=85&s=ef25ef0a7ad0c2985928651085d3a8e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/elizalabs/bbIJsUzCDybj9a-t/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=bbIJsUzCDybj9a-t&q=85&s=d696503a5eeb5ccddf46a3e2cdce0190)](https://docs.elizaos.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

LLM Providers

OpenAI Plugin

[Docs](https://docs.elizaos.ai/)
[REST Reference](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference/agents/create-a-new-agent)
[CLI Reference](https://docs.elizaos.ai/cli-reference/overview)
[Plugin Registry](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/overview)
[Launch Resources](https://docs.elizaos.ai/launch-resources)

On this page

*   [Features](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#features)
    
*   [Installation](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#installation)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#configuration)
    
*   [Environment Variables](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#environment-variables)
    
*   [Character Configuration](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#character-configuration)
    
*   [Supported Operations](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#supported-operations)
    
*   [Model Configuration](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#model-configuration)
    
*   [Usage Example](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#usage-example)
    
*   [Cost Considerations](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#cost-considerations)
    
*   [External Resources](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#external-resources)
    

The OpenAI plugin provides access to GPT models and supports all model types: text generation, embeddings, and object generation.

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#features)

Features
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Full model support** - Text, embeddings, and objects
*   **Multiple models** - GPT-4, GPT-3.5, and embedding models
*   **Streaming support** - Real-time response generation
*   **Function calling** - Structured output generation

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#installation)

Installation
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    elizaos plugins add @elizaos/plugin-openai
    

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#configuration)

Configuration
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#environment-variables)

Environment Variables

Copy

Ask AI

    # Required
    OPENAI_API_KEY=sk-...
    
    # Optional model configuration
    # You can use any available OpenAI model
    OPENAI_SMALL_MODEL=gpt-4o-mini        # Default: gpt-4o-mini
    OPENAI_LARGE_MODEL=gpt-4o             # Default: gpt-4o
    OPENAI_EMBEDDING_MODEL=text-embedding-3-small  # Default: text-embedding-3-small
    
    # Examples of other available models:
    # OPENAI_SMALL_MODEL=gpt-3.5-turbo
    # OPENAI_LARGE_MODEL=gpt-4-turbo
    # OPENAI_LARGE_MODEL=gpt-4o-2024-11-20
    # OPENAI_EMBEDDING_MODEL=text-embedding-3-large
    # OPENAI_EMBEDDING_MODEL=text-embedding-ada-002
    

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#character-configuration)

Character Configuration

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "name": "MyAgent",
      "plugins": ["@elizaos/plugin-openai"],
      "settings": {
        "secrets": {
          "OPENAI_API_KEY": "sk-..."
        }
      }
    }
    

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#supported-operations)

Supported Operations
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Operation | Models | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- |
| TEXT\_GENERATION | Any GPT model (gpt-4o, gpt-4, gpt-3.5-turbo, etc.) | Conversational AI |
| EMBEDDING | Any embedding model (text-embedding-3-small/large, ada-002) | Vector embeddings |
| OBJECT\_GENERATION | All GPT models | JSON/structured output |

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#model-configuration)

Model Configuration
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The plugin uses two model categories:

*   **SMALL\_MODEL**: Used for simpler tasks, faster responses
*   **LARGE\_MODEL**: Used for complex reasoning, better quality

You can configure any available OpenAI model in these slots based on your needs and budget.

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#usage-example)

Usage Example
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The plugin automatically registers with the runtime:

Copy

Ask AI

    // No manual initialization needed
    // Just include in plugins array
    

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#cost-considerations)

Cost Considerations
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   GPT-4 is more expensive than GPT-3.5
*   Use `text-embedding-3-small` for cheaper embeddings
*   Monitor usage via OpenAI dashboard

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openai#external-resources)

External Resources
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [Plugin Source](https://github.com/elizaos/eliza/tree/main/packages/plugin-openai)
    
*   [OpenAI API Documentation](https://platform.openai.com/docs)
    
*   [Pricing](https://openai.com/pricing)

YesNo

[Anthropic Plugin](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/anthropic)

# OpenRouter Plugin - ElizaOS Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#content-area)

[ElizaOS Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/elizalabs/bbIJsUzCDybj9a-t/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=bbIJsUzCDybj9a-t&q=85&s=ef25ef0a7ad0c2985928651085d3a8e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/elizalabs/bbIJsUzCDybj9a-t/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=bbIJsUzCDybj9a-t&q=85&s=d696503a5eeb5ccddf46a3e2cdce0190)](https://docs.elizaos.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

LLM Providers

OpenRouter Plugin

[Docs](https://docs.elizaos.ai/)
[REST Reference](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference/agents/create-a-new-agent)
[CLI Reference](https://docs.elizaos.ai/cli-reference/overview)
[Plugin Registry](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/overview)
[Launch Resources](https://docs.elizaos.ai/launch-resources)

On this page

*   [Features](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#features)
    
*   [Installation](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#installation)
    
*   [Configuration](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#configuration)
    
*   [Environment Variables](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#environment-variables)
    
*   [Character Configuration](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#character-configuration)
    
*   [Supported Operations](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#supported-operations)
    
*   [Important: Embedding Fallback](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#important%3A-embedding-fallback)
    
*   [Model Configuration](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#model-configuration)
    
*   [Premium Models](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#premium-models)
    
*   [Open Models](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#open-models)
    
*   [Pricing Strategy](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#pricing-strategy)
    
*   [External Resources](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#external-resources)
    

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#features)

Features
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Multiple providers** - Access 50+ models from various providers
*   **Automatic failover** - Route to available providers
*   **Cost optimization** - Choose models by price/performance
*   **Single API key** - One key for all providers

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#installation)

Installation
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    elizaos plugins add @elizaos/plugin-openrouter
    

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#configuration)

Configuration
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#environment-variables)

Environment Variables

Copy

Ask AI

    # Required
    OPENROUTER_API_KEY=sk-or-...
    
    # Optional model configuration
    # You can use any model available on OpenRouter
    OPENROUTER_SMALL_MODEL=google/gemini-2.0-flash-001           # Default: google/gemini-2.0-flash-001
    OPENROUTER_LARGE_MODEL=google/gemini-2.5-flash-preview-05-20 # Default: google/gemini-2.5-flash-preview-05-20
    OPENROUTER_IMAGE_MODEL=anthropic/claude-3-5-sonnet           # For vision tasks
    
    # Examples of other available models:
    # OPENROUTER_SMALL_MODEL=anthropic/claude-3-haiku
    # OPENROUTER_LARGE_MODEL=anthropic/claude-3-opus
    # OPENROUTER_LARGE_MODEL=openai/gpt-4o
    # OPENROUTER_SMALL_MODEL=meta-llama/llama-3.1-8b-instruct:free
    

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#character-configuration)

Character Configuration

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "name": "MyAgent",
      "plugins": [\
        "@elizaos/plugin-openrouter",\
        "@elizaos/plugin-ollama"  // For embeddings\
      ]
    }
    

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#supported-operations)

Supported Operations
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Operation | Support | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- |
| TEXT\_GENERATION | ✅   | All available models |
| EMBEDDING | ❌   | Use fallback plugin |
| OBJECT\_GENERATION | ✅   | Model dependent |

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#important%3A-embedding-fallback)

Important: Embedding Fallback
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

OpenRouter doesn’t provide embedding endpoints, so include a fallback:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "plugins": [\
        "@elizaos/plugin-openrouter",  // Text generation\
        "@elizaos/plugin-openai"        // Embeddings\
      ]
    }
    

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#model-configuration)

Model Configuration
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The plugin uses model tiers:

*   **SMALL\_MODEL**: Fast, cost-effective responses
*   **LARGE\_MODEL**: Complex reasoning, best quality
*   **IMAGE\_MODEL**: Multimodal capabilities

OpenRouter provides access to 50+ models from various providers. You can use:

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#premium-models)

Premium Models

*   Any Anthropic Claude model (Opus, Sonnet, Haiku)
*   Any OpenAI GPT model (GPT-4o, GPT-4, GPT-3.5)
*   Google Gemini models (Pro, Flash, etc.)
*   Cohere Command models

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#open-models)

Open Models

*   Meta Llama models (3.1, 3.2, 3.3)
*   Mistral/Mixtral models
*   Many models with `:free` suffix for testing

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#pricing-strategy)

Pricing Strategy
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

OpenRouter charges a small markup (usually ~10%) on top of provider prices:

1.  **Pay-per-token** - No monthly fees
2.  **Price transparency** - See costs per model
3.  **Credits system** - Pre-pay for usage

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/openrouter#external-resources)

External Resources
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [Plugin Source](https://github.com/elizaos/eliza/tree/main/packages/plugin-openrouter)
    
*   [OpenRouter Documentation](https://openrouter.ai/docs)
    
*   [Model List & Pricing](https://openrouter.ai/models)

YesNo

[Ollama Plugin](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/llm/ollama)

Summary
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Knowledge plugin’s architecture is designed for:

Scalability
-----------

Handles large document collections efficiently

Performance
-----------

Optimized processing and retrieval paths

Reliability
-----------

Robust error handling and recovery

Cost Efficiency
---------------

90% savings with intelligent caching

Understanding these flows helps you:

*   Optimize configuration for your use case
*   Debug issues effectively
*   Plan for scale
*   Integrate with other systems

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/testing-guide#testing-philosophy)

Testing Philosophy
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Test with small amounts on mainnet. Solana devnet/testnet tokens have no value and often have different behavior than mainnet.

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/testing-guide#safe-testing-practices)

Safe Testing Practices
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/testing-guide#1-start-small)

1\. Start Small

Test with minimal amounts:

*   0.001 SOL for transfers (~$0.20)
*   $1-5 worth of tokens for swaps
*   Use common tokens (USDC, USDT) for reliability

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/testing-guide#2-transaction-costs)

2\. Transaction Costs

Solana transactions are cheap (~$0.00025 per transaction), making mainnet testing affordable.

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/testing-guide#3-progressive-testing)

3\. Progressive Testing

Copy

Ask AI

    1. Check wallet connection
    2. Test SOL transfers
    3. Test SPL token transfers  
    4. Test small swaps
    5. Test larger operations
    

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/testing-guide#testing-checklist)

Testing Checklist
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/testing-guide#environment-setup)

Environment Setup

Copy

Ask AI

    # Use a dedicated test wallet
    SOLANA_PRIVATE_KEY=test_wallet_private_key
    
    # Optional - Use premium RPC for reliability
    SOLANA_RPC_URL=https://mainnet.helius-rpc.com/?api-key=YOUR_KEY
    

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/testing-guide#basic-tests)

Basic Tests

1.  **Wallet Connection**
    
    Copy
    
    Ask AI
    
        User: What's my wallet address?
        Agent: [Should show your Solana address]
        
    
2.  **Balance Check**
    
    Copy
    
    Ask AI
    
        User: What's my balance?
        Agent: [Should show SOL balance and token holdings]
        
    
3.  **Small SOL Transfer**
    
    Copy
    
    Ask AI
    
        User: Send 0.001 SOL to [another address]
        Agent: [Should execute the transfer]
        
    
4.  **Token Transfer**
    
    Copy
    
    Ask AI
    
        User: Send 1 USDC to [test address]
        Agent: [Should handle SPL token transfer]
        
    

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/testing-guide#swap-testing)

Swap Testing

Test swaps with small amounts:

Copy

Ask AI

    User: Swap 0.1 SOL for USDC
    Agent: [Should execute via Jupiter]
    

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/testing-guide#portfolio-tracking)

Portfolio Tracking

Copy

Ask AI

    User: What's my portfolio worth?
    Agent: [Should show total USD value and token breakdown]
    

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/testing-guide#monitoring-results)

Monitoring Results
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Transaction Verification**
    *   Check on Solscan.io or Solana Explorer
    *   Verify transaction succeeded
    *   Confirm balance changes
2.  **Common Token Addresses**
    *   USDC: EPjFWdd5AufqSSqeM2qN1xzybapC8G4wEGGkZwyTDt1v
    *   USDT: Es9vMFrzaCERmJfrF4H2FYD4KCoNkY11McCe8BenwNYB
    *   Use these for testing as they’re widely supported

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/testing-guide#common-issues)

Common Issues
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/testing-guide#%E2%80%9Dinsufficient-sol-for-fees%E2%80%9D)

”Insufficient SOL for fees”

*   Need ~0.001 SOL for transaction fees
*   Keep some SOL for rent and fees

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/testing-guide#%E2%80%9Dtoken-account-doesn%E2%80%99t-exist%E2%80%9D)

”Token account doesn’t exist”

*   First transfer to a new token creates the account
*   Costs ~0.002 SOL for account creation

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/testing-guide#%E2%80%9Dslippage-tolerance-exceeded%E2%80%9D)

”Slippage tolerance exceeded”

*   Increase slippage for volatile tokens
*   Try smaller amounts

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/testing-guide#production-readiness)

Production Readiness
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before production use:

1.  Test all operations you plan to use
2.  Verify error handling
3.  Test with your expected token types
4.  Monitor transaction success rates
5.  Set appropriate slippage (1-3% typical)
6.  Ensure adequate SOL for fees

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Examples](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/examples)

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/examples#configuration)

Configuration
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/examples#character-configuration)

Character Configuration

Add the Solana plugin to your character file:

Copy

Ask AI

    // character.ts
    import { type Character } from '@elizaos/core';
    
    export const character: Character = {
      name: 'SolanaAgent',
      plugins: [\
        // Core plugins\
        '@elizaos/plugin-sql',\
        '@elizaos/plugin-bootstrap',\
        \
        // Solana plugin\
        ...(process.env.SOLANA_PRIVATE_KEY?.trim() ? ['@elizaos/plugin-solana'] : []),\
        \
        // Platform plugins\
        ...(process.env.DISCORD_API_TOKEN?.trim() ? ['@elizaos/plugin-discord'] : []),\
      ],
      settings: {
        secrets: {},
      },
      // ... rest of character configuration
    };
    

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/examples#environment-variables)

Environment Variables

Copy

Ask AI

    # Required - Choose one:
    SOLANA_PRIVATE_KEY=your_base58_private_key_here
    # OR for read-only mode:
    SOLANA_PUBLIC_KEY=your_public_key_here
    
    # Optional - Enhanced RPC
    SOLANA_RPC_URL=https://mainnet.helius-rpc.com/?api-key=YOUR_KEY
    HELIUS_API_KEY=your_helius_key
    
    # Optional - Market data
    BIRDEYE_API_KEY=your_birdeye_key
    

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/examples#usage-examples)

Usage Examples
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/examples#transfer-operations)

Transfer Operations

The agent understands natural language for transfers:

Copy

Ask AI

    User: Send 1 SOL to 7xKXtg2CW87d97TXJSDpbD5jBkheTqA83TZRuJosgAsU
    Agent: I'll send 1 SOL to that address right away.
    
    User: Transfer 100 USDC to alice.sol
    Agent: Transferring 100 USDC to alice.sol.
    
    User: Pay bob 50 BONK tokens
    Agent: Sending 50 BONK to bob.
    

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/examples#swap-operations)

Swap Operations

Copy

Ask AI

    User: Swap 10 SOL for USDC
    Agent: I'll swap 10 SOL for USDC using Jupiter.
    
    User: Exchange all my BONK for SOL
    Agent: Swapping all your BONK tokens for SOL.
    
    User: Trade 100 USDC for JTO with 2% slippage
    Agent: Swapping 100 USDC for JTO with 2% slippage tolerance.
    

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/examples#portfolio-management)

Portfolio Management

Copy

Ask AI

    User: What's my wallet balance?
    Agent: [Shows total portfolio value and individual token balances]
    
    User: How much is my portfolio worth?
    Agent: Your total portfolio value is $X,XXX.XX (XX.XX SOL)
    

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/examples#custom-plugin-integration)

Custom Plugin Integration
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you need to import the plugin directly in a ProjectAgent:

Copy

Ask AI

    // index.ts
    import { type ProjectAgent } from '@elizaos/core';
    import solanaPlugin from '@elizaos/plugin-solana';
    import { character } from './character';
    
    export const projectAgent: ProjectAgent = {
      character,
      plugins: [solanaPlugin], // Import custom plugins here
      init: async (runtime) => {
        // Custom initialization if needed
      }
    };
    

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/examples#common-patterns)

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/examples#domain-name-resolution)

Domain Name Resolution

The plugin automatically resolves .sol domains:

Copy

Ask AI

    User: Send 5 SOL to vitalik.sol
    Agent: Sending 5 SOL to vitalik.sol [resolves to actual address]

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/examples#token-symbol-resolution)

Token Symbol Resolution

Common tokens are automatically recognized:

Copy

Ask AI

    User: Send 100 USDC to alice
    Agent: [Recognizes USDC token mint and handles transfer]
    

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/defi/solana/examples#all-balance-swaps)

All Balance Swaps

Copy

Ask AI

    User: Swap all my BONK for USDC

*   [Performance Considerations](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#performance-considerations)
    
*   [Processing Time](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#processing-time)
    
*   [Cost Estimation](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#cost-estimation)

*   [Common Issues and Solutions](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#common-issues-and-solutions)
    
*   [Context Not Being Added](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#context-not-being-added)
    
*   [Slow Processing](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#slow-processing)
    
*   [High Costs](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#high-costs)
    
*   [Best Practices](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#best-practices)
    
*   [Summary](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#summary)
    

Contextual embeddings are an advanced Knowledge plugin feature that improves retrieval accuracy by enriching text chunks with surrounding context before generating embeddings. This implementation is based on [Anthropic’s contextual retrieval techniques](https://www.anthropic.com/news/contextual-retrieval)
.

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#what-are-contextual-embeddings%3F)

What are Contextual Embeddings?
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Traditional RAG systems embed isolated text chunks, losing important context. Contextual embeddings solve this by using an LLM to add relevant context to each chunk before embedding.

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#traditional-vs-contextual)

Traditional vs Contextual

*   Traditional Embedding
    
*   Contextual Embedding
    

Copy

Ask AI

    Original chunk:
    "The deployment process requires authentication."
    
    Embedded as-is, missing context about:
    - Which deployment process?
    - What kind of authentication?
    - For which system?
    

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#how-it-works)

How It Works
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Knowledge plugin uses a sophisticated prompt-based approach to enrich chunks:

1.  **Document Analysis**: The full document is passed to an LLM along with each chunk
2.  **Context Generation**: The LLM identifies relevant context from the document
3.  **Chunk Enrichment**: The original chunk is preserved with added context
4.  **Embedding**: The enriched chunk is embedded using your configured embedding model

The implementation is based on Anthropic’s Contextual Retrieval cookbook example, which showed up to 50% improvement in retrieval accuracy.

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#configuration)

Configuration
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#enable-contextual-embeddings)

Enable Contextual Embeddings

.env

Copy

Ask AI

    # Enable contextual embeddings
    CTX_KNOWLEDGE_ENABLED=true
    
    # Configure your text generation provider
    TEXT_PROVIDER=openrouter  # or openai, anthropic, google
    TEXT_MODEL=anthropic/claude-3-haiku  # or any supported model
    
    # Required API keys
    OPENROUTER_API_KEY=your-key  # If using OpenRouter
    # or
    OPENAI_API_KEY=your-key      # If using OpenAI
    # or
    ANTHROPIC_API_KEY=your-key   # If using Anthropic
    # or  
    GOOGLE_API_KEY=your-key      # If using Google
    

**Important**: Embeddings always use the model configured in `useModel(TEXT_EMBEDDING)` from your agent setup. Do NOT try to mix different embedding models - all your documents must use the same embedding model for consistency.

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#recommended-setup%3A-openrouter-with-separate-embedding-provider)

Recommended Setup: OpenRouter with Separate Embedding Provider

Since OpenRouter doesn’t support embeddings, you need a separate embedding provider:

*   OpenRouter + OpenAI
    
*   OpenRouter + Google
    

character.ts

Copy

Ask AI

    export const character = {
      name: 'MyAgent',
      plugins: [\
        '@elizaos/plugin-openrouter',  // For text generation\
        '@elizaos/plugin-openai',       // For embeddings\
        '@elizaos/plugin-knowledge',    // Knowledge plugin\
      ],
    };
    

.env

Copy

Ask AI

    # Enable contextual embeddings
    CTX_KNOWLEDGE_ENABLED=true
    
    # Text generation (for context enrichment)
    TEXT_PROVIDER=openrouter
    TEXT_MODEL=anthropic/claude-3-haiku
    OPENROUTER_API_KEY=your-openrouter-key
    
    # Embeddings (automatically used)
    OPENAI_API_KEY=your-openai-key
    

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#alternative-providers)

Alternative Providers

*   OpenAI Only
    
*   Anthropic + OpenAI
    
*   Google Only
    
*   OpenRouter + Google
    

Copy

Ask AI

    CTX_KNOWLEDGE_ENABLED=true
    TEXT_PROVIDER=openai
    TEXT_MODEL=gpt-4o-mini
    OPENAI_API_KEY=your-key
    

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#technical-details)

Technical Details
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#chunk-processing)

Chunk Processing

The plugin uses fixed chunk sizes optimized for contextual enrichment:

*   **Chunk Size**: 500 tokens (approximately 1,750 characters)
*   **Chunk Overlap**: 100 tokens
*   **Context Target**: 60-200 tokens of added context

These values are based on research showing that smaller chunks with rich context perform better than larger chunks without context.

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#content-aware-templates)

Content-Aware Templates

The plugin automatically detects content types and uses specialized prompts:

Copy

Ask AI

    // Different templates for different content types
    - General text documents
    - PDF documents (with special handling for corrupted text)
    - Mathematical content (preserves equations and notation)
    - Code files (includes imports, function signatures)
    - Technical documentation (preserves terminology)
    

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#openrouter-caching)

OpenRouter Caching

When using OpenRouter with Claude or Gemini models, the plugin automatically leverages caching:

1.  **First document chunk**: Caches the full document
2.  **Subsequent chunks**: Reuses cached document (90% cost reduction)
3.  **Cache duration**: 5 minutes (automatic)

This means processing a 100-page document costs almost the same as processing a single page!

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#example%3A-how-context-improves-retrieval)

Example: How Context Improves Retrieval
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#without-contextual-embeddings)

Without Contextual Embeddings

Copy

Ask AI

    Query: "How do I configure the timeout?"
    
    Retrieved chunk:
    "Set the timeout value to 30 seconds."
    
    Problem: Which timeout? Database? API? Cache?
    

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#with-contextual-embeddings)

With Contextual Embeddings

Copy

Ask AI

    Query: "How do I configure the timeout?"
    
    Retrieved chunk:
    "In the Redis configuration section, when setting up the caching layer,
    set the timeout value to 30 seconds for optimal performance with 
    session data."
    
    Result: Clear understanding this is about Redis cache timeout.
    

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#performance-considerations)

Performance Considerations
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#processing-time)

Processing Time

*   **Initial processing**: 1-3 seconds per chunk (includes LLM call)
*   **With caching**: 0.1-0.3 seconds per chunk
*   **Batch processing**: Up to 30 chunks concurrently

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#cost-estimation)

Cost Estimation

| Document Size | Pages | Chunks | Without Caching | With OpenRouter Cache |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Small | 10  | ~20 | $0.02 | $0.002 |
| Medium | 50  | ~100 | $0.10 | $0.01 |
| Large | 200 | ~400 | $0.40 | $0.04 |

Costs are estimates based on Claude 3 Haiku pricing. Actual costs depend on your chosen model.

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#monitoring)

Monitoring
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The plugin provides detailed logging:

Copy

Ask AI

    # Enable debug logging to see enrichment details
    LOG_LEVEL=debug elizaos start
    

This will show:

*   Context enrichment progress
*   Cache hit/miss rates
*   Processing times per document
*   Token usage

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#common-issues-and-solutions)

Common Issues and Solutions
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#context-not-being-added)

Context Not Being Added

**Check if contextual embeddings are enabled:**

Copy

Ask AI

    # Look for this in your logs:
    "CTX enrichment ENABLED"
    # or
    "CTX enrichment DISABLED"
    

**Verify your configuration:**

*   `CTX_KNOWLEDGE_ENABLED=true` (not “TRUE” or “True”)
*   `TEXT_PROVIDER` and `TEXT_MODEL` are both set
*   Required API key for your provider is set

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#slow-processing)

Slow Processing

**Solutions:**

1.  Use OpenRouter with Claude/Gemini for automatic caching
2.  Process smaller batches of documents
3.  Use faster models (Claude 3 Haiku, Gemini 1.5 Flash)

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#high-costs)

High Costs

**Solutions:**

1.  Enable OpenRouter caching (90% cost reduction)
2.  Use smaller models for context generation
3.  Process documents in batches during off-peak hours

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#best-practices)

Best Practices
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

Use OpenRouter for Cost Efficiency

OpenRouter’s caching makes contextual embeddings 90% cheaper when processing multiple chunks from the same document.

2

Keep Default Settings

The chunk sizes and overlap are optimized based on research. Only change if you have specific requirements.

3

Monitor Your Logs

Enable debug logging when first setting up to ensure context is being added properly.

4

Use Appropriate Models

*   Claude 3 Haiku: Best balance of quality and cost
*   Gemini 1.5 Flash: Fastest processing
*   GPT-4o-mini: Good quality, moderate cost

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/knowledge/contextual-embeddings#summary)

Summary
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Contextual embeddings significantly improve retrieval accuracy by:

*   Adding document context to each chunk before embedding
*   Using intelligent templates based on content type
*   Preserving the original text while enriching with context
*   Leveraging caching for cost-efficient processing

The implementation is based on Anthropic’s proven approach and integrates seamlessly with elizaOS’s existing infrastructure. Simply set `CTX_KNOWLEDGE_ENABLED=true` and configure your text generation provider to get started!

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

The @elizaos/plugin-discord enables your elizaOS agent to operate as a Discord bot with full support for messages, voice channels, slash commands, and media processing.

🔧 Configuration
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/platform/discord#required-settings)

Required Settings

*   `DISCORD_APPLICATION_ID` - Your Discord application ID
*   `DISCORD_API_TOKEN` - Bot authentication token

### 

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/plugin-registry/platform/discord#optional-settings)

Optional Settings

*   `CHANNEL_IDS` - Restrict bot to specific channels
*   `DISCORD_VOICE_CHANNEL_ID` - Default voice channel

# REST Reference - ElizaOS Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference#content-area)

[ElizaOS Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/elizalabs/bbIJsUzCDybj9a-t/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=bbIJsUzCDybj9a-t&q=85&s=ef25ef0a7ad0c2985928651085d3a8e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/elizalabs/bbIJsUzCDybj9a-t/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=bbIJsUzCDybj9a-t&q=85&s=d696503a5eeb5ccddf46a3e2cdce0190)](https://docs.elizaos.ai/)

REST Reference

[Docs](https://docs.elizaos.ai/)
[REST Reference](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference/agents/create-a-new-agent)

On this page

*   [Core APIs](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference#core-apis)
    
*   [Media & Audio](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference#media-%26-audio)
    
*   [System & Monitoring](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference#system-%26-monitoring)
    
*   [Getting Started](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference#getting-started)
    
*   [API Standards](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference#api-standards)
    
*   [Need Help?](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference#need-help%3F)
    

Welcome to the elizaOS REST Reference. This comprehensive guide covers all available REST endpoints and services for building and managing AI agents.

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference#core-apis)

Core APIs
------------------------------------------------------------------

[Agents\
------\
\
Create, manage, and control AI agents. Handle agent lifecycle, configuration, and world management.](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference/agents/create-a-new-agent)
[Messaging\
---------\
\
Real-time messaging system for agent communication. Create servers, channels, and manage conversations.](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference/messaging/create-server)
[Memory\
------\
\
Agent memory management. Store, retrieve, and organize agent memories and contextual information.](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference/memory/get-agent-memories)
[Rooms\
-----\
\
Virtual spaces for agent interactions. Create and manage rooms for organized conversations.](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference/rooms/create-a-room)

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference#media-%26-audio)

Media & Audio
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Audio\
-----\
\
Speech synthesis, transcription, and audio processing capabilities.](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference/audio/generate-speech-from-text)
[Media\
-----\
\
Media upload and management for agents and channels.](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference/media/upload-media-for-agent)

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference#system-%26-monitoring)

System & Monitoring
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[System\
------\
\
System status, health checks, and server management endpoints.](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference/system/basic-health-check)
[Logs\
----\
\
Logging and debugging tools for agents and system operations.](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference/logs/get-agent-logs)
[WebSocket\
---------\
\
Real-time WebSocket connections for live agent interactions.](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference/websocket/socketio-real-time-connection)

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference#getting-started)

Getting Started
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

Authentication

Set up your API credentials and authentication tokens.

2

Create an Agent

Use the [Create Agent endpoint](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference/agents/create-a-new-agent)
 to start building.

3

Configure Messaging

Set up [messaging channels](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference/messaging/create-channel)
 for agent communication.

4

Test Integration

Use [health check endpoints](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference/system/basic-health-check)
 to verify your setup.

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference#api-standards)

API Standards
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

All API endpoints follow RESTful conventions:

*   **GET** - Retrieve resources
*   **POST** - Create new resources
*   **PUT** - Update existing resources
*   **DELETE** - Remove resources

Response formats are consistently JSON with appropriate HTTP status codes.

[​](https://docs.elizaos.ai/rest-reference#need-help%3F)
